10 نکته ای که باید در مورد لباسشویی بدانید
اگر به دنبال خرید ماشین لباسشویی هستید، مهم است که بدانید به چه چیزی نیاز دارید و چه نوع ماشین هایی در دسترس است. بنابراین قبل از اینکه بیرون بروید و ماشین لباسشویی خود را به خانه ببرید، در اینجا 10 نکته وجود دارد که باید در مورد ماشینی که می‌خرید بدانید.
1. آیا این دستگاه نیمه اتوماتیک است یا تمام اتوماتیک؟
این به نیازها و محدودیت های بودجه شما بستگی دارد.
تفاوت ماشین لباسشویی نیمه اتوماتیک و ماشین لباسشویی اتوماتیک را در مقالات دیگر ما ببینید
تنظیمات شستشو بسیاری از ماشین های لباسشویی تمام اتوماتیک برنامه های مختلفی را برای شستشوهای مختلف مانند لباس های ظریف یا پشمی ارائه می دهند. برخی از آنها را می توان سفارشی کرد و حتی می توانید تنظیمات دلخواه خود را ذخیره کنید تا آنها را در دسترس داشته باشید.
2. هنگام خرید ماشین لباسشویی به دنبال چه ویژگی هایی هستید؟
چرخش چرخشی. بسته به پارچه و نوع لباسی که می خواهید
چرخه شستشو و چرخش، برحسب دور در دقیقه بیان می شود.
اقلام ظریف مهم باید فقط در مرکز چرخه با سرعت خشک شدن 300-500 دور، زمان قرار داده شوند.
برخی از سخت ها می توانند تا 1000 دور در دقیقه بروند.
4. بهره وری هنگام خرید لباسشویی
3. ماشین لباسشویی شما چقدر در صرفه جویی در مصرف برق و آب کارآمد است؟
یک ماشین لباسشویی اقتصادی به معنای صرفه جویی در طولانی مدت است.
5. اندازه ماشین لباسشویی
ماشین های بارگیری از بالا نسبت به ماشین های لباسشویی تمام اتوماتیک درب جلو باریک تری دارند. آیا باید ماشین لباسشویی خود را در گوشه ای تنگ قرار دهید؟ یا شما می توانید
فضای اضافی را در نظر بگیرید، موارد بزرگتر به ماشین لباسشویی بزرگتری نیاز دارند
بارگذاری می شود که ما را به نقطه بعدی می رساند.
6. ظرفیت بار ماشین لباسشویی
اگر
شما خانواده پرجمعیتی دارید و ماشین لباسشویی می خواهید
یک بار بزرگ، بر خلاف یک خانواده کوچک یا یک فرد مجرد
7. آیا ماشین لباسشویی خشک کن دارد؟
اگر زندگی پرمشغله ای دارید و زمانی برای شستن لباس ندارید، ماشین لباسشویی با خشک کن داخلی می تواند انتخاب خوبی برای شما باشد.
8. آیا درام از فولاد ساخته شده است یا پلاستیک؟
لوازم جانبی درام ماشین لباسشویی می تواند وارد آن شود
انواع پلاستیک مانند روکش های فولادی ضد زنگ یا چینی؛
با فولاد که نسخه گران تر و بادوام تر است.
9. در از بالاست یا جلو؟
ماشین آلات درب بالا و جلو مزایا و معایب زیادی دارند.
شما می توانید در مورد تفاوت بین دستگاه بارگیری از بالا یا جلو در مقاله ما بخوانید.
10. آیا می توان از پیش کلاهک کرد؟
اگر کودکی دارید که دوست دارد کثیف شود یا مشکل دارد
بسیاری از لکه های سخت ممکن است نیاز به خیساندن داشته باشند که می توان با استفاده از برنامه خیساندن این کار را انجام داد
برای تعمیر ماشین ظرفشویی بوش در تهران به لینک زیر مراجعه نمایید.
https://paydarservice.org/تعمیر-ماشین-ظرفشویی-بوش/

Parafialny zespół Caritas
admin
Celem Caritas Parafii jest szerzenie chrześcijańskich zasad charytatywnych, bezpośrednia działalność charytatywna, jednoczenie, koordynowanie i kierowanie kościelną akcją charytatywną na terenie parafii oraz współpraca z innymi wyznaniowymi, a także niekościelnymi instytucjami i formami pomocy wzajemnej.
Zadaniami Caritas Parafii są w szczególności:
1. Mobilizacja charytatywna całej wspólnoty Ludu Bożego w parafii do praktykowania miłosierdzia modlitwą, słowem i czynem, w szczególności poprzez:
* kultywowanie parafialnych i rodzinnych zwyczajów charytatywnych,
* przygotowywanie akcji charytatywnych,
* uroczyste obchodzenie świąt charytatywnych.
2. W miarę pełne i stałe rozpoznawanie potrzeb i możliwości pomocy charytatywnej na terenie parafii, przy czym nie należy wykluczać możliwości rozszerzenia pomocy, w miarę istniejących środków, poza teren parafii.
3. Organizowanie i świadczenie konkretnej pomocy osobom potrzebującym, a w szczególności:
rodzinom, w szczególności wielodzietnym,
osobom chorym, w podeszłym wieku i niepełnosprawnym,
dzieciom i młodzieży zaniedbanej,
osobom ubogim i przeżywającym inne trudności życiowe.
Wszystkich zainteresowanych włączeniem się w dzieło
Sporządził: Wojciech Bernaś
Sprawozdanie Parafialnego Zespołu Caritas za:
2023 rok
2022 rok
2021 rok
2020 rok

Buick
December 7th, 2006 Alex Leave a comment Go to comments
I did get the Buick towed to Performance Motorsports last week. The motor is seized. Marshall was looking around for an inexpensive replacement. Found one for $650 with a 90 day warranty and a refurb with factory warranty would be around $2k. So he is taking apart the motor to see if it is something simple that can be replaced. Awaiting word from the man.

Alison Fielden & Co. | Solicitors & Notary Public | Legal Aid

Alison Fielden & Co. - Legal Aid
Alison Fielden & Co is a long standing legal aid practice with a commitment to access to justice for all. We have a legal aid contract in Family Law.
Legal aid is no longer available in many family cases.
There are some exceptions. Legal aid is still available in the following circumstances:
If you are in dispute with social services about your children, for example if social services are trying to remove your children from your home and you wish to contest this.
For victims of domestic violence
In cases of international child abduction, where your partner is trying to take your child out of the UK, or has already done so
If your child is being taken into care by social services.
However, there is no legal aid available for divorce, children or finance cases unless you are going through mediation or you can prove that you are a victim of domestic violence. You may also be eligible for legal aid in divorces where your child is at risk of abuse by another person.
To get legal aid in these circumstances, you MUST produce evidence. We cannot get this evidence for you.
For a list of evidence required to claim legal aid, see this document.
At your first interview, you MUST also bring photo ID and up-to-date evidence of ALL your income. This includes EVERY bank or other account in which you have an interest.
IMPORTANT - What you MUST bring:
Photo ID
Up-to-date evidence of ALL your income and capital (please refer to the checklist here)
Evidence of eligibility (see above)
You can check if you are financially eligible for Legal Aid with the GOV.UK Legal Aid Checker.
We are very sorry but if you come for your first interview without your photo ID, full and up-to-date financial details and the required evidence of domestic violence or child abuse, we cannot see you. You may then have to wait up to two months for another appointment. So please read the requirements carefully - and call or email us if you are unsure what is required - so you don't miss out.

Dog Impulse Control: 4 Exercises for Better Behavior
Do you wish your dog would do things like have patience and wait for you? This is known as impulse control and many dog owners wish their dog had more of it, therefore if that includes you, you’re not alone.
There are lots of benefits to your pet having better treatments for their impulses.
By teaching your dog impulse control, you are able to help your pet to become a well-mannered and easy-going pup.
What Would be the Benefits of Dog Impulse Control?
Impulse control could be best referred to as self-control for your dog. Teaching your pet to have self-control can be quite useful in many situations.
Impulse control helps your pet to learn to hold back patiently for things that they may want. It can also help them learn to stay calm when something thrilling happens. Impulse control is a superb and very simple behavior that you could teach any dog.
These are the main reasons that you may wish to teach your pet impulse control.
Exercises that you can do to Improve your Dog's Impulse Control
These are a few exercise and training tips that you could try to help teach your pet impulse control. It might take some patience on your part to teach them, but by following some of these simple commands, your pet can learn to wait and be patient.
Exercise 1: Crate and Doorway Rushing
Some dogs always desire to be the first with the door. This exercise can help teach your dog to wait and let you feel the door after which follow you thru.
When you first go into the area in which you have your dog's crate or when you’re about to feel the doorway, provide your dog a few minutes to settle down and become calm.
Once they are settled, ask your dog to sit down or lie down.
When your pet is sitting or laying, slowly open the door or even the crate.
If your pet gets as much as go through the door, close the door and get them to sit or lay down.
Repeat, trying to open the door. If your dog gets up, put them back into the sit or down position.
At first, you may want to repeat these steps often before your pet will remain within the desired position until you have opened the doorway. As the dog’s training progresses, the number of times that your dog will have to be reminded in which to stay the correct position will decrease.
Once you will find the door open, provide your dog their release command and allow them to come through the door.
Exercise 2: Place a Treat in your Fist
Put your dog treat, like a piece kibble, in your fists. Put your fist having a treat inside it in front of your canine's nose.
Your dog will try to paw, lick, and sniff at the fist to get at the treat, but do not surrender. Just ignore their attempts to attempt to obtain the treat.
Once your dog has stopped attempting to attack your hand for treats, give them a break having a treat out of your contrary. Once you discover that the dog starts to leave your fist alone when they're presented with the treat in the closed fist, after that you can proceed to the next step.
Now show your pet your fist with dog treats in it. When the dog ignores your fist using the treat, slowly open you to show them the treats. If your dog rushes you when you open your fist, quickly close your fist. When your dog leaves your open hand full of cookies alone, provide them with a goody in the opposite hand. Once your dog can consistently leave the treats inside your open hand alone, you can then move on to the next step.
With your fist open showing your dog the treat, take a treat from the open hand, and give the treat to your dog. If your dog quickly rushes for the treat, close your fist. When your dog begins to patiently wait for you to provide them with the treat, they are able to then receive their reward.
Exercise 3: Waiting for Their Meal
Put your pet in a sit or perhaps a down position and reward with a treat.
Slowly begin to place the food bowl before your dog. When they get up or lunge for the food bowl, stand support and put your dog back into a sit or down position. Then attempt to place the bowl on the floor again.
Once you can put the bowl on the floor, cover the bowl with your hands. In case your dog begins to try to nudge at your hands for that food, keep covering their bowl. If your dog stays within their laying down or sitting position, slowly remove your hands from the bowl. In case your dog lunges for the bowl, cover the bowl back up together with your hands and check out again.
Once you can place the bowl on the ground and uncover it, without your dog moving from the sitting or down position, you are able to give the release command and permit these to eat.
Exercise 4: Awaiting a Treat
Put your pet in the sit position and give them a reward.
Have a goody inside your other hand, held several feet right above your dog's head.
Slowly lower your hand using the treat toward your canine's mouth. If your dog ever gets up or lunges for that treat, pull your hand back up and set your dog back in the sit position. Do not give them a reward this time around.
Continue to repeat this motion before you can get you and treat several inches before your dog's mouth. So long as your pet continues to be sitting quietly and waiting, you can give him the treat.
Next, attempt to continue doing this exercise, but with your hand several feet to the side or in front of your dog. Exactly the same rules apply in various directions. If your dog ever gets up and lunges toward the treat, put them during the sit position, and check out again.
Final Thoughts
Teaching your dog to wait patiently for things and obey some simple commands can sort out many situations.
When taking a walk or which makes them dinner, you don't want your dog to be unmanageable.
These are pretty straight forward tips and tricks which you can use to show your pet to be very patient, wait for food and treats, and most importantly, you should use these concepts like a framework for teaching these to behave well.
These can be quite fun exercises that you simply and your dog can work on to have better dog impulse control and make them a much better family member.

If you are all set to begin playing poker on the internet you may find that there are numerous sites that will attempt to get you to select their website. Generally, most people will just want to take the time to play on one poker casino at a time. You will discover that the very best poker rooms will offer plenty of games available for you to play including but not limited to omaha high, texas holdem Poker, and even 7-Card Stud. You may also notice that a couple of the better poker casinos also have complimentary membership as well.
An additional element you most likely will notice in the greatest poker rooms is advice to help those that are just beginning to play poker. Generally casinos will encourage patrons to practice at free tables before they join rooms that play for cash. The best poker rooms also provide a variety of competitions for their gamblers as well. These competitions are awesome opportunities to wager for gigantic pots of money and you will succeed in a wide array of different ways as well.
Excellent customer service is one more trait that you will certainly find in the greatest poker card rooms. The best sites will provide customer support that is open at all times. Not only will client service give useful assistance but many casinos will provide customers incentives that offer bonus fortunes and sometimes even free money to their members.
Online poker can be great amusement, specifically if you discover the best poker rooms to play in. There is no longer any need to have to drive to a casino when you are able to gamble on poker from the coziness of your house. Why not get begin today and see what the best poker rooms have to present you?

Шутеры
Отличительные черты видео-слота «Lord Of The Ocean»
Октябрь 4th, 2016
«Lord of the Ocean» – это один из тех немногих виртуальных игровых аппаратов, атмосфера которого завораживает геймеров с первых же секунд после начала игры. Он позволяет всем азартным пользователям оказаться в древнейшей и невыразимо прекрасной цивилизации.
Специалисты компании «Novomatic» осмелились разработать по-настоящему захватывающий сюжет, воплощённый в удивительном графическом исполнении игрового аппарата. Поросший непослушными зелёными водорослями остов затерянного в океане корабля, полуразрушенные строения, стиль которых напоминает о некогда величественной Греции, различные животные и стайки рыбок всех цветов радуги – всё то великолепие, что ждёт игроков в этом слоте.
Особенности.
Впрочем, техническое оснащение выбранного нами слота также выполнено на уровне. Игровой аппарат имеет 5 барабанов и 10 линий выплат. Предельная ставка на линию при этом равна 5 кредитам.
Главная роль в игре отведена двум фигурам, а именно — «дикому» символу и символу «разброса». В качестве первого выступает сам Посейдон (у римлян — Нептун). Он ловко дополняет своим появлением любые комбинации. В качестве второго взято изображение знаменитых Врат Посейдона. Этот знак поражает своим могуществом. Он может спокойно игнорировать правила, соединяясь в комбинации с фигурами любых задействованных линий слота. А ещё в игровом аппарате «Lord of the Ocean», доступном для игры в игровом зале Вулкан на сайте vulkan.hall777.com/, присутствуют изображения сундуков, полных сокровищами, древних рун, окаменелых стражников и, конечно же, главной чаровницы океанских глубин – царице подводного мира.
Дополнительная игра с Посейдоном.
Чтобы проверить себя и свою удачу в дополнительном (бонусном) раунде, предлагаемым виртуальным слотом, следует собрать на игровом поле 3 фигуры, изображающие Врата Посейдона. Скаттеры позволят «выбрать» «дикую» фигуру специально для дополнительного раунда и подарят десять вращений. Тур далеко не всегда завершается по окончании движения барабанов. «Что это значит?» — поинтересуется недоумевающий геймер. А значит это то, что Скаттеры могут собраться перед удивлённым взором игрока снова. Тем самым они увеличат количество бесплатных вращений и, следовательно, умножат шансы на крупный выигрыш.
Опубликовано в рубрике Симуляторы

居歪 の 目。: 『開箱』Sony Xperia L 火紅開箱！
居歪 の 目。
機身：Sony a55。 鏡頭：16-105、35mm f1.8、18-55。
2013-12-13
『開箱』Sony Xperia L 火紅開箱！
於： 19:46
將將！好久不見的電子產品開箱文，
是的，自從決定要存錢換手機跟換相機之後，文具病這種東西就像驅邪過了一樣消失了，
最近這一陣子應該只有瘋狂觀測相機手機的動向哈！
不囉嗦來開箱！
這不是手誤發錯！也不是裝笑為！
這是前兩年換的手機：hTC Sensation XE 參見。
這陣子他老了，很容易頓，大家說是換顆電池或者刷機就可以讓他回春，
但我實在很懶，而且手機約也要到了就決定是中華電信辦支手機來！
挑了一枝物美價廉的手機，Sony Xperia L
選擇的是大省方案３３３，這樣只要$2990
關於大省方案就自己去google吧！
神腦提供一年保固，外包裝只有白色，所以大家拿貨的時候不要以為店員在耍你，
背面才有顯示3個顏色，但他也不會告訴你理頭裝什麼顏色XD
要從盒底看才知道，不過這方面就交給店員去煩惱就好。
開開開開箱~~~
當然不是第一次開，初開箱在中華電信就被豪邁的割開包裝，還割到下面去= =+
所以上上張圖是上下兩段膠帶都給割開了XD
手機擺的位置蠻抖的，就這樣放著也沒有特別保護，
雖然說包裝盒是蠻堅固的啦，但堅固的外盒跟堅固的手機撞來撞去不就很...
但近年來的手機似乎都這樣，當初XE不也是這樣~(攤手)
拎出手機本人以即一堆哩哩叩叩的物件，
送了Hami Apps 其中兩個，防護軟體只是個廣告根本沒有送 (小氣啦中華電信
而亮點就是這張轉接卡~
大概是最近手機大卡小卡霧煞煞，就特別付上轉接卡讓小卡的民眾可以無痛轉接
其實這樣也不錯，乾脆以後大家都辦小卡，手機付轉接卡就好啦~
不然卡換來換去好煩，買空機的話還要自己跑一趟電信去換卡 (碎碎念)
辦門號就沒這煩惱了~直接換一換就好，轉接卡的部分也可以在中華電信取得。
話說我這次辦了小卡，因為這支手機不是要給我用的XD
我換的手機要用小卡~然後中華電信也直接送我轉接卡，但我也不知道是不是有辦卡就可以免費拿到~
扯回開箱，盒內的其他配件很簡潔
旅充頭、傳輸線、沒用的耳機 (以後可以不要送這個，然後便宜個$50好嗎)
吐槽完所有配件後，終於可以來看本體了!!!
我選的是紅通通的紅，說是紅通通也只有背蓋是紅的
螢幕4.3吋，沒有實體鍵，只有俗稱海苔條的首頁、返回、視窗
手機邊框是鋼琴烤漆 (螢幕以外的黑色部分)，所以會沾指紋。
背蓋的部分是摸起來跟XE背蓋很相的霧面膠感，會挑L也是因為這樣就可以裸機了XD
好討厭會沾指紋的背蓋，又討厭用保護殼什麼的，
整體看起來就是中規中矩，但說老實話我會比較喜歡早期的Xperia系列的樣子 (再度碎碎念)
側面部分，電源鍵在右側，最近的SONY機器都移到這一側
我覺得蠻方便也挺順手的，但就是這個鈕很醜而已。
(右側下方有拍照實體鍵，忘記拍了)
左側，從這邊打開手機，
但我覺得有沒有凹槽根本無所謂，可以直接從頂上的斜面往下輕輕扳就打開了，
不用死命的去摳壓那個凹槽。
拆下後~
(電池正常是在包裝內的，因為我去中華電信買現場就直接裝上了)
左側背蓋上搭載最近很紅的NFC晶片。
(蘋果頗跩的說他們不需要NFC 用藍芽就好了)
不過NFC也是經過感應去連藍芽的啦，所以也是沒差~蘋果開心就好 (持續碎碎念)
拆下電池，可以看到Xperia L是支援裝置記憶卡的，最大可擴充至32G
電池的部分是1700mAh而已，
對愛打電動的人來說應該是非常不足~就帶尿袋行動電源或者第二顆電池吧！
鏡頭部分(800萬畫素)，
但有略研究相機的人都知道畫素只是浮雲，只能當參考不能當作全部標準來看，
另配置一補光燈。
背面看完就闔上去吧！
剛才從頭上拆，所以現在從屁股裝回去。
盒上其實就有告訴你怎麼拆、裝
左邊那張圖是拆，右邊那張圖是裝。
來開機啦~
SONY LOGO，回歸SONY比較好
雖然骨子裡還是有易利信的血，但隨便我不在意。
開機動畫，打燈比較不明顯
關掉閃燈拍拍，
這個動畫讓我媽讚賞了一番，說是很好看(?)
我是覺得普通還好而已XD
854 x 480pixels 解析度的 TFT 觸控螢幕
這...比XE還差哈
雖說整體規格不到很多大師的標準，但對初入智慧機或者需求不高的民眾來講已經是綽綽有餘了。
外型算好看也是大廠，搭配門號的價格低廉，即便是買空機也不過5、6千，蠻值得的了
而維修部分呢，住在大台北以外的民眾可能就會辛苦一點，
因為SONY的維修是外包的，不像hTC是到府收件，所以要自己親自跑一趟維修部門，或者是請電信行代為送修。
(我是比較推薦台北市府維修站(我去修過相機，服務不錯也很快速)，其他沒去過就不知道了)
總之呢，不好也不壞的將將好手機就是了呢！
我只是開開箱而已～測試跑分什麼我就不是很在行了
請大家另求google大師指點啦！
說到這了，其實這支手機也不是我要用的~
本來是要跟媽媽換SV來用的，但一拿到SONY才發現跟hTC差太多了，
不是說SONY差，是使用習慣問題，所以Xperia L 回到我手中，但我也沒要用 L 所以最後又被我賣出了XD
到底我要換哪支手機呢?!
可能要過一陣子才知道了呢~~~
但我的XE也賣掉了就是了，正在用一台不知道怎麼形容的Desire C撐著撐著...

Главная / Акции / Ящики для сбора пожертвований
Опубликовано 08.06.2017 23.01.2018 от Максим Гильнич
Ящики для сбора пожертвований
Ящик для сбора денег фанерный
Новые ящики для пожертвований производятся из двух типов материалов. Для изготовления лицевой прозрачной части используется высококачественный ударопрочный пластик, который отличается от оргстекла особой прочностью. Боковые стенки и задняя панель выполнены из шлифованной фанеры толщиной 4 миллиметра.
Размер ШхВхГ мм 235х245х170 / Размер информатора (А-4)
Цена — 1875 рублей
Ящик для пожертвований
Самый недорогой и практичный ящик для пожертвований. Используется для провидения различных акций и сбора пожертвований. Имеет прорезь для документов и купюр размером -130х4мм (возможно изменение положения прорези). Защитный элемент, установленный на купюро-приёмнике, благодаря своей конструкции исключает кражу денег. Изготовлено методом высокоточной фрезерной резки и термогибки из лучшего из сортов пластика — литого поликарбоната (не оргстекло!), устойчивого к ударам, механическим и химическим воздействиям. Под заказ — нужный Вам размер и цвет пластика, а также нанесение изображения на лицевую сторону ящика методом печати на прозрачной виниловой плёнке с последующей аппликацией.
Размер Ш/В/Г мм — 230х290х180
Цена — 1530 рублей
Ящик для сбора пожертвований с информатором А4
Материал
Акрил 3 мм. Акрил 2 мм. Болты 30 шт. Замок 1 шт.
Размер
ширина-350мм, высота-300мм, глубина-300мм, карман А4 горизонтальный
Цена — 5946 рублей
Коробка для денег
Материал
Акрил 3 мм. Акрил 2 мм. Пэт Болты 38 шт. Замок 1 шт.
Размер
ширина-420мм, высота-420мм, глубина-300мм.
Цена — 6645 руб
Ящик для пожертвований на пластиковой тумбе
Обращаем Ваше внимание, что подставка для ящика (тумба) может быть выполнена в различной цветовой гамме, а также возможна имитация фактур — дерева, камня, металла, ткани и др. виниловыми плёнками.
Комплектация:
ящик для пожертвований на тумбе — 1шт, замок врезной — 1шт, ключ — 2шт.
Размер Ш/В/Г мм 320х1550х250 Толщина прозрачного ударопрочного пластика 2 мм, Толщина белого ударопрочного пластика 3 мм
Цена — 10200 руб

a MÁFIA portuguesa: ADVOGADOS ABANDONAM SALA NA TOMADA DE POSSE DO BASTONÁRIO
skip to main | skip to sidebar
ADVOGADOS ABANDONAM SALA NA TOMADA DE POSSE DO BASTONÁRIO
Marinho Pinto odiado por alguns, apoiado por muitos, pelo seu estilo frontal de falar
Grande parte dos membros eleitos do Conselho Superior da Ordem dos Advogados (OA), e parte dos membros cessantes do mesmo órgão, num total de cerca de 20 pessoas, abandonaram ontem à noite a tomada de posse do Bastonário. António Marinho Pinto, eleito a 26 de Novembro com 49% dos votos, recordou no discurso de posse do seu 2.º mandato à frente da Orde dos Advogados, os seis processos disciplinares de que foi alvo nos dois primeiros anos do primeiro triénio a que presidiu ao organismo. “Alguns destes processos foram verdadeiras ignomínias quanto aos seu motivos. O Conselho Superior da OA agiu como polícia, Ministério público, e Juiz em relação ao Bastonário. Chegou a apelar-se publicamente à apresentação de queixas contra o Bastonário”, recordou. Mal tinha acabado de proferir estas palavras, o Bastonário era confrontado com uma revolta do Conselho Superior da OA. O primeiro a abandonar a sala foi José António Barreiros, presidente cessante do Conselho Superior, no que foi seguido, em solidariedade, por vice-presidentes do actual órgão, e do que ontem cessou funções. Rodolfo Lavrador, membro fundador da OA, e vice-presidente eleito no actual Conselho Superior, disse ao CM que abandonava a sala por não “pactuar com mentiras”. Marinho Pinto comentou esta manifestação, desvalorizando-a, e referindo que a mesma veio de “quem sabe que foi autor de mentiras”.

輪之流

輪之流
作者: 林息敏
分類: 其他
更新: 9小時前
加入書架
開始閱讀
早在一千多年前，在遙遠的北方
衍生出一種人麵獸耳的生物，他們有著毛絨絨的尾巴和異於常人的能力…
生性古怪難以捉摸
因怪異的能力和外貌，他們有了一個稱呼，名叫‘幻靈狐’
而正是因為它們的出現，人類近乎滅絕，整個天下由這神秘的種族主導
隨著勢力逐漸龐大，人類開始反抗，一場大戰拉開帷幕…
而在這場戰爭中，而‘它’是幻靈狐族萬千人中的一員，卻不幸受傷，生命危在旦夕，而此時，天空中卻出現了一道光圈…故事的序章就此開始

喬心笙裴承州
對裴律師亂撩後，她攜崽出逃了！
上輩子，喬心笙被摯愛和最信任的養女妹妹聯手害死。冇曾想，重生後的第一個病患竟是渣妹那權勢滔天的白月光？剛好，這輩子她就想手撕渣男賤女，順便撩撩這位矜貴的男人。運氣好，把他撩到手，氣死妹妹，再不濟，也能噁心一下妹妹。奈何這禁慾男人是真的難撩：“喬醫生，彆撩不該撩的人，你玩不起。”挫敗的她打算抽身，誰知道卻被他堵住：“喬醫生，撩完就跑，不用負責？”後來……有人親眼看到，那位矜貴的裴律師掐著她的腰，帶著敲骨吸髓的狠勁吻她。後來，喬心笙發現這狗男人根本冇病。“裴承州，你就是個騙子！”“喬醫生，是你誤診了。”（1v1，重生逆襲爽文）
娛樂：種地劁豬，這真是小糊咖
肖宇
肖宇是個即將告彆娛樂圈的小糊咖 隨著種地綜藝的大火，肖宇頂替了同公司的蔡鯤鯤參加了一檔叫做《種地吧！大明星！》的真人秀綜藝 公司本想著讓肖宇在退圈前替蔡坤坤去這個綜藝湊數，卻冇想到這個糊到地心的小鮮肉居然讓全國網友都震驚了 “他自己一口氣卸下了三十多噸有機肥，這特麼是小鮮肉？” “手持小鐵刀，一刀便劁豬，又穩又狠，震驚全場” “說好的好吃懶做，可人家一個人就能置辦流水席” “敢說肖宇眼睛瞎，他的眼睛就是尺，分毫不差！” 看著一個又一個的熱搜衝上了圍脖，經紀公司都懵逼了！ 這特麼還是那個卑微至極的小糊咖嗎？合作電話都打爆了！ （本書內容及出場人物均屬杜撰，如有雷同，純屬巧合！）
林舟許念初小說免費聽
林舟許念初
【重生+戀愛+單女主+腦洞+狗糧+賺錢】林舟死了。奮鬥半生，他事業有成，家財萬貫，是令人羨慕的鑽石王老五。可死後才知道，孤單一生的他，連葬禮都冇人辦。多麼可笑啊。後來，他看見一個女人衝進了病房。看見她抱著他的遺體哭的撕心裂肺。看見她親手給他整理了儀容，辦了葬禮。又帶著他曾經無意間送她的禮物，跳了河……那一刻，林舟才知道。原來有人那麼努力的深愛著他……重生一世，看著坐在自己身邊，膽小又可愛的小同桌。林舟笑了。“許念初，你好，我是林舟，你未來的……愛人。”

Abstract
Singularities of robot manipulators have been intensely studied in the last decades by researchers of many fields. Serial singularities produce some local loss of dexterity of the manipulator, therefore it might be desirable to search for singularityfree trajectories in the jointspace. On the other hand, parallel singularities are very dangerous for parallel manipulators, for they may provoke the local loss of platform control, and jeopardize the structural integrity of links or actuators. It is therefore utterly important to avoid parallel singularities, while operating a parallel machine. Furthermore, there might be some configurations of a parallel manipulators that are allowed by the constraints, but nevertheless are unreachable by any feasible path. The present work proposes a numerical procedure based upon Morse theory, an important branch of differential topology. Such procedure counts and identify the singularity-free regions that are cut by the singularity locus out of the configuration space, and the disjoint regions composing the configuration space of a parallel manipulator. Moreover, given any two configurations of a manipulator, a feasible or a singularity-free path connecting them can always be found, or it can be proved that none exists. Examples of applications to 3R and 6R serial manipulators, to 3UPS and 3UPU parallel wrists, to 3UPU parallel translational manipulators, and to 3RRR planar manipulators are reported in the work.
